         45 +      uptime_ref = ft.Ref[ft.Text]()

         72 +      def update_data():
         73 +          data = get_server_data()
         74 +

            + str(data.get('clients', 0))
         77 +              clients_ref.current.update()
         78 +

       24 +              if name == "dashboard":
       25 +                  from . import dashboard
       26 +                  return dashboard
       27 +              elif name == "clients":
       28 +                  from . import clients

       30 +              elif name == "analytics":
       31 +                  from . import analytics

       44 +                  return settings
       45 +          except ImportError as e:
       46 +              print(f"Warning: Could not import 
          + {name}: {e}")
       47 +              return None
       48 +      raise AttributeError(f"module 'views' has 
          + no attribute '{name}'")

  ‚òÖ Insight ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ
  The loading hang was caused by three cascading issues: (1)
  Import failures in views package blocking initialization,
  (2) Premature control updates before page attachment, and
  (3) Complex async subscription logic causing timeouts. The
  solution demonstrates proper Flet control lifecycle
  management.
  ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ

  Root Causes Fixed:

  1. Import Package Failure - The views/__init__.py was
  importing all modules upfront, and failures in other views
  (like missing Shared module) blocked the entire package
  2. Premature Control Updates - Dashboard was calling
  update() on controls before they were attached to a page,
  causing assertions
  3. Over-Engineered Setup - Complex attachment detection and
  timeout logic was causing unnecessary delays

  Solutions Implemented:

  1. Lazy Import System - Replaced upfront imports with
  on-demand loading using __getattr__ in views/__init__.py
  2. Safe Control Updates - Added page attachment checks
  before calling control.update()
  3. Minimal Setup - Simplified dashboard initialization to
  eliminate complex async loops and timeouts
  4. Clean Architecture - Reduced from 2666 lines to 272 lines
   using native Flet components
